bootdelaykey=   
fdt_high=0x2000000

loadaddr=0x4000000

configurationname=newtec/swconfig.dat
remoteenvname=newtec/remoteenv.dat

bootcmd=echo ''; run bootcmdpre && run boottftp; run bootcmdfail
bootcmdpre=setenv bootargs ${bootargs} uboot=\\\\\\"${ver}\\\\\\"; run loadfpga && fpgabr 1 && run postfpgacmd && run factory_reset && run post_ramtest
bootcmdfail=echo --BOOT FAILED--; echo Reset and retry in ${failwaittime}s ...; sleep ${failwaittime} && reset
bootargs=console=ttyS0,115200 rootfstype=squashfs,ext2 root=/dev/ram0 debug
failwaittime=5

useremoteenv=if test -n "${remoteenvver}"; then env set ver "${ver}+${remoteenvver}"; fi; if test -n "${remoteenvcmd}"; then echo --RUN remoteenvcmd--; run remoteenvcmd; fi; true

loadcmdcore=echo --LOAD FPGA--; tftp ${serverip}:${fpgacorename} && fpga loadfs 0 mem 0 ${loadaddr} core

i. ARP Tables
-------------

arptables v0.0.3-4: can't initialize arptables table `filter': arptables who? (do you need to insmod?)
Perhaps arptables or your kernel needs to be upgraded.
